生成された Formura 全文(polar2d.fmr・28 行) 
dimension :: 3
axes :: r,phi,z

double :: dt = 0.0001

extern function :: cos
extern function :: exp

begin function (u,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3,FormuraeInternalMetricVolume) = init()
  double [] :: u, FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1, FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2, FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3, FormuraeInternalMetricVolume
  u[i,j,k] = exp((-2) + (-4) * (dr * i)**2 + 4 * dr * i + cos(dphi * j))
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1[i,j,k] = 1 + dr * ((1 / 2) + i)
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2[i,j,k] = (1 + dr * i) / (1 + dr * i)**2
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3[i,j,k] = 1 + dr * i
  FormuraeInternalMetricVolume[i,j,k] = 1 + dr * i
end function

begin function (u',FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1',FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2',FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3',FormuraeInternalMetricVolume') = step(u,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3,FormuraeInternalMetricVolume)
  FormuraeInternalLb1Flux1[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1[i,j,k] * (u[i+1,j,k] + (-1) * u[i,j,k]) / dr
  FormuraeInternalLb1Flux2[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2[i,j,k] * (u[i,j+1,k] + (-1) * u[i,j,k]) / dphi
  FormuraeInternalLb1Flux3[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3[i,j,k] * (u[i,j,k+1] + (-1) * u[i,j,k]) / dz
  FormuraeInternalLb1Result[i,j,k] = ((FormuraeInternalLb1Flux1[i,j,k] + (-1) * FormuraeInternalLb1Flux1[i-1,j,k]) / dr + (FormuraeInternalLb1Flux2[i,j,k] + (-1) * FormuraeInternalLb1Flux2[i,j-1,k]) / dphi + (FormuraeInternalLb1Flux3[i,j,k] + (-1) * FormuraeInternalLb1Flux3[i,j,k-1]) / dz) / FormuraeInternalMetricVolume[i,j,k]
  u'[i,j,k] = u[i,j,k] + dt * FormuraeInternalLb1Result[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricVolume'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricVolume[i,j,k]
end function
左: 実際の円環上に描いた u(t=0.2)/右: (r,φ) チャート
独立参照実装と 5.6e-16・Σr·u 保存 1.1e-15・最大値原理成立。

球座標の球殻(3D)

Δu = (1/r²)∂r(r²∂ru) + (1/r²sinθ)∂θ(sinθ∂θu) + (1/r²sin²θ)∂φφu
Formurae ソース全文(spherical3d.fme・26 行) 
-- Heat equation in FULL 3D SPHERICAL COORDINATES, on a shell:
-- (r_phys, theta_phys, phi) = (1 + r, 1 + theta, phi),
-- r_phys in [1, 2], theta_phys in [1, 1 + L] (poles avoided).
-- All three axes are nontrivial.  From the embedding the CAS derives
-- g = diag(1, (1+r)^2, (1+r)^2 sin^2(1+theta)) -- the spherical
-- Laplacian -- checks orthogonality symbolically, and assembles the
-- conservative flux form.  Both r and theta walls are Neumann
-- (mirror), phi is periodic.

mode collocated
dimension 3
axes r, θ, φ

param dt = 0.0002

def Δ u = lb u

embedding [ `(1 + r) * sin (1 + θ) * cos φ, `(1 + r) * sin (1 + θ) * sin φ, `(1 + r) * cos (1 + θ) ]

field u : scalar

init:
  u := exp (0 - 4 * (r - 1 / 2) ^ 2) * exp (0 - 4 * (θ - 1 / 2) ^ 2) * exp (cos φ - 1)

step:
  u' = u + dt * Δ u

dimension :: 3
axes :: r,theta,phi

double :: dt = 0.0002

extern function :: sin
extern function :: cos
extern function :: exp

begin function (u,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3,FormuraeInternalMetricVolume) = init()
  double [] :: u, FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1, FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2, FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3, FormuraeInternalMetricVolume
  u[i,j,k] = exp((-3) + (-4) * (dr * i)**2 + (-4) * (dtheta * j)**2 + 4 * dr * i + 4 * dtheta * j + cos(dphi * k))
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1[i,j,k] = 2 * dr * ((1 / 2) + i) * sin(1 + dtheta * j) + (dr * ((1 / 2) + i))**2 * sin(1 + dtheta * j) + sin(1 + dtheta * j)
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2[i,j,k] = (2 * dr * i * sin(1 + dtheta * ((1 / 2) + j)) + (dr * i)**2 * sin(1 + dtheta * ((1 / 2) + j)) + sin(1 + dtheta * ((1 / 2) + j))) / (1 + dr * i)**2
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3[i,j,k] = (2 * dr * i * sin(1 + dtheta * j) + (dr * i)**2 * sin(1 + dtheta * j) + sin(1 + dtheta * j)) / (dr * i * sin(1 + dtheta * j) + sin(1 + dtheta * j))**2
  FormuraeInternalMetricVolume[i,j,k] = 2 * dr * i * sin(1 + dtheta * j) + (dr * i)**2 * sin(1 + dtheta * j) + sin(1 + dtheta * j)
end function

begin function (u',FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1',FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2',FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3',FormuraeInternalMetricVolume') = step(u,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3,FormuraeInternalMetricVolume)
  FormuraeInternalLb1Flux1[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1[i,j,k] * (u[i+1,j,k] + (-1) * u[i,j,k]) / dr
  FormuraeInternalLb1Flux2[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2[i,j,k] * (u[i,j+1,k] + (-1) * u[i,j,k]) / dtheta
  FormuraeInternalLb1Flux3[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3[i,j,k] * (u[i,j,k+1] + (-1) * u[i,j,k]) / dphi
  FormuraeInternalLb1Result[i,j,k] = ((FormuraeInternalLb1Flux1[i,j,k] + (-1) * FormuraeInternalLb1Flux1[i-1,j,k]) / dr + (FormuraeInternalLb1Flux2[i,j,k] + (-1) * FormuraeInternalLb1Flux2[i,j-1,k]) / dtheta + (FormuraeInternalLb1Flux3[i,j,k] + (-1) * FormuraeInternalLb1Flux3[i,j,k-1]) / dphi) / FormuraeInternalMetricVolume[i,j,k]
  u'[i,j,k] = u[i,j,k] + dt * FormuraeInternalLb1Result[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricVolume'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricVolume[i,j,k]
end function
左: 外殻面 r=2 上の u(t=0.2)/右: (r,θ) 断面
独立 3D 参照実装と 4.4e-16・Σr²sinθ·u 保存 4.2e-15・最大値原理成立。

計量つき拡散(トーラス上の Laplace–Beltrami)

∂tu = (1/√g) ∂i(√g gij ∂ju)
トーラス R=2, r=1: √g = 2+cos θ, gθθ=1, gφφ=1/(2+cos θ)²
Formurae ソース全文(metric_torus.fme・31 行) 
-- Heat equation on a curved surface (a torus), from the COORDINATES:
-- the embedding of the (theta, phi, z) chart into R^4 below is the
-- only geometric input.  The compiler differentiates it (CAS), forms
-- the metric g_ab = dX/dx_a . dX/dx_b, checks orthogonality
-- symbolically (generation is gated on g_12 = g_13 = g_23 = 0),
-- takes the scale factors h_a = sqrt(g_aa), evaluates the hodge
-- factors sqrt(g)/h_a^2 at the half-cell placements, freezes them
-- into coefficient fields, and exposes lb u as an
-- exactly conservative flux form.
--
-- Backquotes keep `(2 + cos θ) atomic during the CAS work
-- (sin^2 + cos^2 collapses to 1, sqrt of the quoted square reduces),
-- and quote-transparent substitution keeps the reduced factor compact.

mode collocated
dimension 3
axes θ, φ, z

param dt = 0.0005

def Δ u = lb u

embedding [ `(2 + cos θ) * cos φ, `(2 + cos θ) * sin φ, sin θ, z ]

field u : scalar

init:
  u := exp (cos θ + cos φ - 2)

step:
  u' = u + dt * Δ u

  let actualVariances := Formurae.logicalTensorVariances value
      actualDegree := dfOrder value
      exactMetadata := actualVariances = variances && actualDegree = degree
      completesOmittedDownIndices := degree = 0
                                      && actualDegree > 0
                                      && actualVariances = variances
   in match assert "normalized equation tensor metadata mismatch"

        | #True -> FEIR.encodeTensorWithMetadata feParameters feCoordinatesRegistry feFields feIntrinsics feAnalytics variances degree value

生成された Formura 全文(metric_torus.fmr・28 行) 
dimension :: 3
axes :: theta,phi,z

double :: dt = 0.0005

extern function :: cos
extern function :: exp

begin function (u,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3,FormuraeInternalMetricVolume) = init()
  double [] :: u, FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1, FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2, FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3, FormuraeInternalMetricVolume
  u[i,j,k] = exp((-2) + cos(dphi * j) + cos(dtheta * i))
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1[i,j,k] = 2 + cos(dtheta * ((1 / 2) + i))
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2[i,j,k] = (2 + cos(dtheta * i)) / (2 + cos(dtheta * i))**2
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3[i,j,k] = 2 + cos(dtheta * i)
  FormuraeInternalMetricVolume[i,j,k] = 2 + cos(dtheta * i)
end function

begin function (u',FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1',FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2',FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3',FormuraeInternalMetricVolume') = step(u,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3,FormuraeInternalMetricVolume)
  FormuraeInternalLb1Flux1[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1[i,j,k] * (u[i+1,j,k] + (-1) * u[i,j,k]) / dtheta
  FormuraeInternalLb1Flux2[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2[i,j,k] * (u[i,j+1,k] + (-1) * u[i,j,k]) / dphi
  FormuraeInternalLb1Flux3[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3[i,j,k] * (u[i,j,k+1] + (-1) * u[i,j,k]) / dz
  FormuraeInternalLb1Result[i,j,k] = ((FormuraeInternalLb1Flux1[i,j,k] + (-1) * FormuraeInternalLb1Flux1[i-1,j,k]) / dtheta + (FormuraeInternalLb1Flux2[i,j,k] + (-1) * FormuraeInternalLb1Flux2[i,j-1,k]) / dphi + (FormuraeInternalLb1Flux3[i,j,k] + (-1) * FormuraeInternalLb1Flux3[i,j,k-1]) / dz) / FormuraeInternalMetricVolume[i,j,k]
  u'[i,j,k] = u[i,j,k] + dt * FormuraeInternalLb1Result[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricVolume'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricVolume[i,j,k]
end function
左: トーラス上に描いた u(t=3000、陰影つき 3D)/右: (θ,φ) チャート
独立 C 参照と 3.3e-16(全桁一致)・計量重みつき熱量 Σ√g·u 保存 2.5e-15・ 最大値原理成立。スケール因子導出版の .fmr は手展開版とバイト一致。

球面の帯(正曲率)

∂tu = ΔS²u,  余緯度 θ ∈ [1, 1+L] の帯
埋め込みから g=diag(1, sin²θ) を CAS が導出、θ 壁は mirror(Neumann)
Formurae ソース全文(metric_sphere.fme・26 行) 
-- Heat equation on a BAND OF THE UNIT SPHERE (positive curvature),
-- colatitude theta_phys = 1 + theta in [1, 1 + L] (poles avoided).
-- The embedding below is the only geometric input: the compiler
-- derives g = diag(1, sin^2(1+theta)) via the CAS (sin^2+cos^2
-- collapses, sqrt of the square closes), checks orthogonality, and
-- assembles the conservative Laplace-Beltrami flux form.  The theta
-- walls are Neumann (yaml boundary: mirror), so the metric-weighted
-- heat sum(sin(1+theta) u) is exactly conserved.

mode collocated
dimension 3
axes θ, φ, z

param dt = 0.0001

def Δ u = lb u

embedding [ sin (1 + θ) * cos φ, sin (1 + θ) * sin φ, cos (1 + θ), z ]

field u : scalar

init:
  u := exp (0 - 4 * (θ - 1 / 2) ^ 2) * exp (cos φ - 1)

step:
  u' = u + dt * Δ u

def feGeometryMetricRaw := (FE.metricTensor feDimension (FE.inducedMetric feCoordinates feGeometryEmbedding))_formuraeTensorIndex1_formuraeTensorIndex2
def feGeometryScaleRaw axis := sqrt (FE.tensorComponentAt feGeometryMetricRaw [axis, axis])
def feGeometryOrthogonalityVerified : Bool := assert "embedding/metric must be symbolically orthogonal" (FE.tensorComponentAt feGeometryMetricRaw [1,2] = 0 && FE.tensorComponentAt feGeometryMetricRaw [1,3] = 0 && FE.tensorComponentAt feGeometryMetricRaw [2,3] = 0)

  | #True -> feGeometryMetricRaw

  | #True -> feGeometryScaleRaw axis

  | #True -> feGeometryInverseMetricRaw

def FormuraeInternalEncodeTensor expectedShape variances degree value :=
  let actualVariances := Formurae.logicalTensorVariances value
      actualDegree := dfOrder value
      exactMetadata := actualVariances = variances && actualDegree = degree
      completesOmittedDownIndices := degree = 0
                                      && actualDegree > 0
                                      && actualVariances = variances
   in match assert "normalized equation tensor metadata mismatch"
                   (tensorShape value = expectedShape
                    && (exactMetadata || completesOmittedDownIndices)) as bool with
        | #True -> FEIR.encodeTensorWithMetadata feParameters feCoordinatesRegistry feFields feIntrinsics feAnalytics variances degree value

生成された Formura 全文(metric_sphere.fmr・29 行) 
dimension :: 3
axes :: theta,phi,z

double :: dt = 0.0001

extern function :: sin
extern function :: cos
extern function :: exp

begin function (u,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3,FormuraeInternalMetricVolume) = init()
  double [] :: u, FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1, FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2, FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3, FormuraeInternalMetricVolume
  u[i,j,k] = exp((-2) + (-4) * (dtheta * i)**2 + 4 * dtheta * i + cos(dphi * j))
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1[i,j,k] = sin(1 + dtheta * ((1 / 2) + i))
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2[i,j,k] = sin(1 + dtheta * i) / sin(1 + dtheta * i)**2
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3[i,j,k] = sin(1 + dtheta * i)
  FormuraeInternalMetricVolume[i,j,k] = sin(1 + dtheta * i)
end function

begin function (u',FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1',FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2',FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3',FormuraeInternalMetricVolume') = step(u,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3,FormuraeInternalMetricVolume)
  FormuraeInternalLb1Flux1[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1[i,j,k] * (u[i+1,j,k] + (-1) * u[i,j,k]) / dtheta
  FormuraeInternalLb1Flux2[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2[i,j,k] * (u[i,j+1,k] + (-1) * u[i,j,k]) / dphi
  FormuraeInternalLb1Flux3[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3[i,j,k] * (u[i,j,k+1] + (-1) * u[i,j,k]) / dz
  FormuraeInternalLb1Result[i,j,k] = ((FormuraeInternalLb1Flux1[i,j,k] + (-1) * FormuraeInternalLb1Flux1[i-1,j,k]) / dtheta + (FormuraeInternalLb1Flux2[i,j,k] + (-1) * FormuraeInternalLb1Flux2[i,j-1,k]) / dphi + (FormuraeInternalLb1Flux3[i,j,k] + (-1) * FormuraeInternalLb1Flux3[i,j,k-1]) / dz) / FormuraeInternalMetricVolume[i,j,k]
  u'[i,j,k] = u[i,j,k] + dt * FormuraeInternalLb1Result[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricVolume'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricVolume[i,j,k]
end function
左: 球面の帯の上に描いた u(t=0.2)/右: (θ,φ) チャート
独立参照実装と 5.6e-16・Σ√g·u 保存 3.6e-15・最大値原理成立。

双曲平面 — Poincaré 半平面(負曲率)

ds² = (dx² + dy²)/y²,  ΔH²u = y²(uxx + uyy)
Formurae ソース全文(hyperbolic.fme・26 行) 
-- Heat equation on the POINCARE HALF-PLANE (constant NEGATIVE
-- curvature -1): ds^2 = (dx^2 + dy^2) / y_phys^2 with
-- y_phys = 1 + y in [1, 2].  A genuinely non-Euclidean geometry that
-- admits no embedding into R^3, so the metric is given directly by
-- its scale factors; the compiler derives sqrt(g) = 1/(1+y)^2 and the
-- hodge factors (both 1 -- the hyperbolic Laplacian is
-- (1+y)^2 (u_xx + u_yy)) and assembles the conservative flux form.
-- The y walls are Neumann (mirror), x is periodic.

mode collocated
dimension 3
axes x, y, z

param dt = 0.00002

def Δ u = lb u

metric scale [ 1 / (1 + y), 1 / (1 + y), 1 ]

field u : scalar

init:
  u := exp (cos x - 1) * exp (0 - 4 * (y - 1 / 2) ^ 2)

step:
  u' = u + dt * Δ u

生成された Formura 全文(hyperbolic.fmr・28 行) 
dimension :: 3
axes :: x,y,z

double :: dt = 0.00002

extern function :: cos
extern function :: exp

begin function (u,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3,FormuraeInternalMetricVolume) = init()
  double [] :: u, FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1, FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2, FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3, FormuraeInternalMetricVolume
  u[i,j,k] = exp((-2) + (-4) * (dy * j)**2 + 4 * dy * j + cos(dx * i))
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1[i,j,k] = 1 / (1 + 2 * dy * j + (dy * j)**2) / (1 / (1 + dy * j))**2
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2[i,j,k] = 1 / (1 + 2 * dy * ((1 / 2) + j) + (dy * ((1 / 2) + j))**2) / (1 / (1 + dy * ((1 / 2) + j)))**2
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3[i,j,k] = 1 / (1 + 2 * dy * j + (dy * j)**2)
  FormuraeInternalMetricVolume[i,j,k] = 1 / (1 + 2 * dy * j + (dy * j)**2)
end function

begin function (u',FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1',FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2',FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3',FormuraeInternalMetricVolume') = step(u,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2,FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3,FormuraeInternalMetricVolume)
  FormuraeInternalLb1Flux1[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1[i,j,k] * (u[i+1,j,k] + (-1) * u[i,j,k]) / dx
  FormuraeInternalLb1Flux2[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2[i,j,k] * (u[i,j+1,k] + (-1) * u[i,j,k]) / dy
  FormuraeInternalLb1Flux3[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3[i,j,k] * (u[i,j,k+1] + (-1) * u[i,j,k]) / dz
  FormuraeInternalLb1Result[i,j,k] = ((FormuraeInternalLb1Flux1[i,j,k] + (-1) * FormuraeInternalLb1Flux1[i-1,j,k]) / dx + (FormuraeInternalLb1Flux2[i,j,k] + (-1) * FormuraeInternalLb1Flux2[i,j-1,k]) / dy + (FormuraeInternalLb1Flux3[i,j,k] + (-1) * FormuraeInternalLb1Flux3[i,j,k-1]) / dz) / FormuraeInternalMetricVolume[i,j,k]
  u'[i,j,k] = u[i,j,k] + dt * FormuraeInternalLb1Result[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient1[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient2[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricCoefficient3[i,j,k]
  FormuraeInternalMetricVolume'[i,j,k] = FormuraeInternalMetricVolume[i,j,k]
end function
半平面チャート上の u(t=0 → 0.1): 上端(y 大)ほど実効拡散 y² が速い

formurae — Egison (テンソル添字記法+CAS) × Formura (分散ステンシル、temporal blocking)。 すべての数値は make all の検証ドライバが exit code で保証。
